That is about the only thing I have issue with. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8998048 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I am not sure exactly what some of those words are but eventually I want to understand everything. My preconceived notions on what will get people to buy something need to be backed up with numbers and facts. So, I cannot check the boxes yet but that does not meen I wont once I learn about them. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex
